       <div class="block block-nucleus-data odd" id="block-nucleus-data-server-time">
        <script type="text/javascript">
         var currenttime = "June 21, 2018 19:54:04"
                var serverdate= new Date(currenttime)
 
                function padlength(zero) {
                  var output=(zero.toString().length==1)? "0"+zero : zero
                  return output
                }
                function displaytime() {
                  serverdate.setSeconds(serverdate.getSeconds()+1)
                  var timestring = padlength(serverdate.getHours()) + ":" + padlength(serverdate.getMinutes())
                  document.getElementById("footerservertime").innerHTML=timestring
                  if (document.getElementById("servertime")) {
                    document.getElementById("servertime").innerHTML=timestring
                  }
                }
                setInterval("displaytime()", 1000);
        </script>
        <div class="time-block">
         <span id="footerservertime">
         </span>
        </div>
